def test_branch_header(systemId, expectedBranch):
post_data = """<soapenv:Envelope xmlns:q0="http://service.bni.co.id/core" xmlns:bo="http://service.bni.co.id/core/bo" xmlns:soapenv="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">
<soapenv:Body>
<q0:transaction>
<request>
<systemId>${systemId}</systemId>
<customHeader>
<branch>${branch}</branch>
<terminal>210</terminal>
<teller>30011</teller>
<overrideFlag></overrideFlag>
<supervisorId/>
</customHeader>
<content xsi:type="bo:DepositTransferReq">
<fromAccount>9870011691389501</fromAccount>
<toAccount>114479721</toAccount>
<amount>1</amount>
<charge>0</charge>
<currency>IDR</currency>
<narative>aaaa</narative>
<narativeExt/>
<promoCode/>
</content>
</request>
</q0:transaction>
</soapenv:Body>
</soapenv:Envelope>
"""
s = Template(post_data)
req = s.safe_substitute(systemId=systemId, branch=expectedBranch)

# SSH to Server ['ssh', '-i', 'ssh-key.txt', 'root@192.168.231.23', 'tail', '-f', '/opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out']
client = paramiko.SSHClient()
client.load_system_host_keys()
client.connect ('192.168.231.23', key_filename='ssh-key.txt', username='soadev')
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('truncate --size 0 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out')

time.sleep(2)

systemId = 'CUSTODY', expectedBranch = '0987'

@pytest.mark.parametrize('systemId, expectedBranch', [('AUTO-SPAN', '0989'),
('BCC_IVR', '0768'),
('BNIDIRECT', '0989'),
('CUSTODY', '0987'),
('IMS', '0987'),
('KSEI', '0987'),
('NEWIBANK-CORE', '0996'),
('SMS', '0992'),
('SYARIAH', '0992'),
('SISKOHAT', '0992'),
('IBOC', '0766'),
('GLOBS', '0766'),
('KIOSK', '0996'),
('NEWMOBILE-CORE', '0996'),
('AGENT', '0985'),
('AGENT-CORE', '0985'),
('ASABRI', '0760'),
('PERSEKOT', '0996'),
('BULOG', '0992'),
('BULOG_FANY', ''),
('EXT-AXWAY', '0996'),
('EXT-IBM', '0996'),
('EXT-REDHAT', '0996'),
('NEWMOBILE', '0991'),
('GOWEALTH', '0957'),
('FSCM', '0989'),
('API', '0986'),
('ELO', '0996'),
('NEWTASPEN', '0999'),
('ECMS', '0984'),
('BCCVA', '0968'),
('AUTODEBET', '0988')])
def test_branch_header(systemId, expectedBranch):
post_data = """<soapenv:Envelope xmlns:q0="http://service.bni.co.id/core" xmlns:bo="http://service.bni.co.id/core/bo" xmlns:soapenv="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">
<soapenv:Body>
<q0:transaction>
<request>
<systemId>${systemId}</systemId>
<customHeader>
<branch>${branch}</branch>
<terminal>210</terminal>
<teller>30011</teller>
<overrideFlag></overrideFlag>
<supervisorId/>
</customHeader>
<content xsi:type="bo:DepositTransferReq">
<fromAccount>9870011691389501</fromAccount>
<toAccount>114479721</toAccount>
<amount>1</amount>
<charge>0</charge>
<currency>IDR</currency>
<narative>aaaa</narative>
<narativeExt/>
<promoCode/>
</content>
</request>
</q0:transaction>
</soapenv:Body>
</soapenv:Envelope>
"""
s = Template(post_data)
req = s.safe_substitute(systemId=systemId, branch=expectedBranch)

# SSH to Server ['ssh', '-i', 'ssh-key.txt', 'root@192.168.231.23', 'tail', '-f', '/opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out']
client = paramiko.SSHClient()
client.load_system_host_keys()
client.connect ('192.168.231.23', key_filename='ssh-key.txt', username='soadev')
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('truncate --size 0 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out')

time.sleep(2)
# POST DATA to core service
headers = {'Content-type': 'application/xml'}
r = requests.post(url_coreservice_baru, data=req, headers=headers)
logger.debug(str(r.status_code) + '---------' + r.text)

# get The f log!
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('tail -1048576 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out | grep "ADAPTER BYTESTREAM"')

log = ""

for line in stdout:
log = line.strip('\n')

logger.debug(log)
i = log.find('003' + expectedBranch)

> assert(i != -1)
E assert -1 != -1

post_data = """<soapenv:Envelope xmlns:q0="http://service.bni.co.id/core" xmlns:bo="http://service.bni.co.id/core/bo" xmlns:soapenv="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">

<teller>30011</teller>
<overrideFlag></overrideFlag>
<supervisorId/>

<fromAccount>9870011691389501</fromAccount>
<toAccount>114479721</toAccount>

<narativeExt/>
<promoCode/>
</content>
</request>
</q0:transaction>
</soapenv:Body>
</soapenv:Envelope>
"""

def test_branch_header(systemId, expectedBranch):
post_data = """<soapenv:Envelope xmlns:q0="http://service.bni.co.id/core" xmlns:bo="http://service.bni.co.id/core/bo" xmlns:soapenv="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">
<soapenv:Body>
<q0:transaction>
<request>
<systemId>${systemId}</systemId>
<customHeader>
<branch>${branch}</branch>
<terminal>210</terminal>
<teller>30011</teller>
<overrideFlag></overrideFlag>
<supervisorId/>
</customHeader>
<content xsi:type="bo:DepositTransferReq">
<fromAccount>9870011691389501</fromAccount>
<toAccount>114479721</toAccount>
<amount>1</amount>
<charge>0</charge>
<currency>IDR</currency>
<narative>aaaa</narative>
<narativeExt/>
<promoCode/>
</content>
</request>
</q0:transaction>
</soapenv:Body>
</soapenv:Envelope>
"""
s = Template(post_data)
req = s.safe_substitute(systemId=systemId, branch=expectedBranch)

# SSH to Server ['ssh', '-i', 'ssh-key.txt', 'root@192.168.231.23', 'tail', '-f', '/opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out']
client = paramiko.SSHClient()
client.load_system_host_keys()
client.connect ('192.168.231.23', key_filename='ssh-key.txt', username='soadev')
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('truncate --size 0 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out')

time.sleep(2)
# POST DATA to core service
headers = {'Content-type': 'application/xml'}
r = requests.post(url_coreservice_baru, data=req, headers=headers)
logger.debug(str(r.status_code) + '---------' + r.text)

# get The f log!
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('tail -1048576 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out | grep "ADAPTER BYTESTREAM"')

log = ""

for line in stdout:
log = line.strip('\n')

logger.debug(log)
i = log.find('003' + expectedBranch)

@pytest.mark.parametrize('systemId, expectedBranch', [('AUTO-SPAN', '0989'),
('BCC_IVR', '0768'),
('BNIDIRECT', '0989'),
('CUSTODY', '0987'),
('IMS', '0987'),
('KSEI', '0987'),
('NEWIBANK-CORE', '0996'),
('SMS', '0992'),
('SYARIAH', '0992'),
('SISKOHAT', '0992'),
('IBOC', '0766'),
('GLOBS', '0766'),
('KIOSK', '0996'),
('NEWMOBILE-CORE', '0996'),
('AGENT', '0985'),
('AGENT-CORE', '0985'),
('ASABRI', '0760'),
('PERSEKOT', '0996'),
('BULOG', '0992'),
('BULOG_FANY', ''),
('EXT-AXWAY', '0996'),
('EXT-IBM', '0996'),
('EXT-REDHAT', '0996'),
('NEWMOBILE', '0991'),
('GOWEALTH', '0957'),
('FSCM', '0989'),
('API', '0986'),
('ELO', '0996'),
('NEWTASPEN', '0999'),
('ECMS', '0984'),
('BCCVA', '0968'),
('AUTODEBET', '0988')])
def test_branch_header(systemId, expectedBranch):
post_data = """<soapenv:Envelope xmlns:q0="http://service.bni.co.id/core" xmlns:bo="http://service.bni.co.id/core/bo" xmlns:soapenv="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">
<soapenv:Body>
<q0:transaction>
<request>
<systemId>${systemId}</systemId>
<customHeader>
<branch>${branch}</branch>
<terminal>210</terminal>
<teller>30011</teller>
<overrideFlag></overrideFlag>
<supervisorId/>
</customHeader>
<content xsi:type="bo:DepositTransferReq">
<fromAccount>9870011691389501</fromAccount>
<toAccount>114479721</toAccount>
<amount>1</amount>
<charge>0</charge>
<currency>IDR</currency>
<narative>aaaa</narative>
<narativeExt/>
<promoCode/>
</content>
</request>
</q0:transaction>
</soapenv:Body>
</soapenv:Envelope>
"""
s = Template(post_data)
req = s.safe_substitute(systemId=systemId, branch=expectedBranch)

# SSH to Server ['ssh', '-i', 'ssh-key.txt', 'root@192.168.231.23', 'tail', '-f', '/opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out']
client = paramiko.SSHClient()
client.load_system_host_keys()
client.connect ('192.168.231.23', key_filename='ssh-key.txt', username='soadev')
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('truncate --size 0 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out')

time.sleep(2)
# POST DATA to core service
headers = {'Content-type': 'application/xml'}
r = requests.post(url_coreservice_baru, data=req, headers=headers)
logger.debug(str(r.status_code) + '---------' + r.text)

# get The f log!
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('tail -1048576 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out | grep "ADAPTER BYTESTREAM"')

log = ""

for line in stdout:
log = line.strip('\n')

logger.debug(log)
i = log.find('003' + expectedBranch)

> assert(i != -1)
E assert -1 != -1

def test_branch_header(systemId, expectedBranch):
post_data = """<soapenv:Envelope xmlns:q0="http://service.bni.co.id/core" xmlns:bo="http://service.bni.co.id/core/bo" xmlns:soapenv="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">
<soapenv:Body>
<q0:transaction>
<request>
<systemId>${systemId}</systemId>
<customHeader>
<branch>${branch}</branch>
<terminal>210</terminal>
<teller>30011</teller>
<overrideFlag></overrideFlag>
<supervisorId/>
</customHeader>
<content xsi:type="bo:DepositTransferReq">
<fromAccount>9870011691389501</fromAccount>
<toAccount>114479721</toAccount>
<amount>1</amount>
<charge>0</charge>
<currency>IDR</currency>
<narative>aaaa</narative>
<narativeExt/>
<promoCode/>
</content>
</request>
</q0:transaction>
</soapenv:Body>
</soapenv:Envelope>
"""
s = Template(post_data)
req = s.safe_substitute(systemId=systemId, branch=expectedBranch)

# SSH to Server ['ssh', '-i', 'ssh-key.txt', 'root@192.168.231.23', 'tail', '-f', '/opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out']
client = paramiko.SSHClient()
client.load_system_host_keys()
client.connect ('192.168.231.23', key_filename='ssh-key.txt', username='soadev')
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('truncate --size 0 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out')

time.sleep(2)
# POST DATA to core service
headers = {'Content-type': 'application/xml'}
r = requests.post(url_coreservice_baru, data=req, headers=headers)
logger.debug(str(r.status_code) + '---------' + r.text)

# get The f log!
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('tail -1048576 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out | grep "ADAPTER BYTESTREAM"')

log = ""

for line in stdout:
log = line.strip('\n')

logger.debug(log)
i = log.find('003' + expectedBranch)

def test_branch_header(systemId, expectedBranch):
post_data = """<soapenv:Envelope xmlns:q0="http://service.bni.co.id/core" xmlns:bo="http://service.bni.co.id/core/bo" xmlns:soapenv="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">
<soapenv:Body>
<q0:transaction>
<request>
<systemId>${systemId}</systemId>
<customHeader>
<branch>${branch}</branch>
<terminal>210</terminal>
<teller>30011</teller>
<overrideFlag></overrideFlag>
<supervisorId/>
</customHeader>
<content xsi:type="bo:DepositTransferReq">
<fromAccount>9870011691389501</fromAccount>
<toAccount>114479721</toAccount>
<amount>1</amount>
<charge>0</charge>
<currency>IDR</currency>
<narative>aaaa</narative>
<narativeExt/>
<promoCode/>
</content>
</request>
</q0:transaction>
</soapenv:Body>
</soapenv:Envelope>
"""
s = Template(post_data)
req = s.safe_substitute(systemId=systemId, branch=expectedBranch)

# SSH to Server ['ssh', '-i', 'ssh-key.txt', 'root@192.168.231.23', 'tail', '-f', '/opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out']
client = paramiko.SSHClient()
client.load_system_host_keys()
client.connect ('192.168.231.23', key_filename='ssh-key.txt', username='soadev')
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('truncate --size 0 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out')

time.sleep(2)
# POST DATA to core service
headers = {'Content-type': 'application/xml'}
r = requests.post(url_coreservice_baru, data=req, headers=headers)
logger.debug(str(r.status_code) + '---------' + r.text)

# get The f log!
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('tail -1048576 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out | grep "ADAPTER BYTESTREAM"')

log = ""

for line in stdout:
log = line.strip('\n')

logger.debug(log)
i = log.find('003' + expectedBranch)

def test_branch_header(systemId, expectedBranch):
post_data = """<soapenv:Envelope xmlns:q0="http://service.bni.co.id/core" xmlns:bo="http://service.bni.co.id/core/bo" xmlns:soapenv="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">

<q0:transaction>
<request>
<systemId>${systemId}</systemId>
<customHeader>
<branch>${branch}</branch>
<terminal>210</terminal>
<teller>30011</teller>
<overrideFlag></overrideFlag>
<supervisorId/>
</customHeader>
<content xsi:type="bo:DepositTransferReq">
<fromAccount>9870011691389501</fromAccount>
<toAccount>114479721</toAccount>
<amount>1</amount>
<charge>0</charge>
<currency>IDR</currency>
<narative>aaaa</narative>
<narativeExt/>
<promoCode/>
</content>
</request>
</q0:transaction>
</soapenv:Body>
</soapenv:Envelope>
"""
s = Template(post_data)
req = s.safe_substitute(systemId=systemId, branch=expectedBranch)

# SSH to Server ['ssh', '-i', 'ssh-key.txt', 'root@192.168.231.23', 'tail', '-f', '/opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out']
client = paramiko.SSHClient()
client.load_system_host_keys()
client.connect ('192.168.231.23', key_filename='ssh-key.txt', username='soadev')
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('truncate --size 0 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out')

time.sleep(2)
# POST DATA to core service
headers = {'Content-type': 'application/xml'}
r = requests.post(url_coreservice_baru, data=req, headers=headers)
logger.debug(str(r.status_code) + '---------' + r.text)

# get The f log!
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('tail -1048576 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out | grep "ADAPTER BYTESTREAM"')

log = ""

for line in stdout:
log = line.strip('\n')

logger.debug(log)
i = log.find('003' + expectedBranch)

def test_branch_header(systemId, expectedBranch):
post_data = """<soapenv:Envelope xmlns:q0="http://service.bni.co.id/core" xmlns:bo="http://service.bni.co.id/core/bo" xmlns:soapenv="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance">
<soapenv:Body>
<q0:transaction>
<request>
<systemId>${systemId}</systemId>
<customHeader>
<branch>${branch}</branch>
<terminal>210</terminal>
<teller>30011</teller>
<overrideFlag></overrideFlag>
<supervisorId/>
</customHeader>
<content xsi:type="bo:DepositTransferReq">
<fromAccount>9870011691389501</fromAccount>
<toAccount>114479721</toAccount>
<amount>1</amount>
<charge>0</charge>
<currency>IDR</currency>
<narative>aaaa</narative>
<narativeExt/>
<promoCode/>
</content>
</request>
</q0:transaction>
</soapenv:Body>
</soapenv:Envelope>
"""
s = Template(post_data)
req = s.safe_substitute(systemId=systemId, branch=expectedBranch)

# SSH to Server ['ssh', '-i', 'ssh-key.txt', 'root@192.168.231.23', 'tail', '-f', '/opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out']
client = paramiko.SSHClient()
client.load_system_host_keys()
client.connect ('192.168.231.23', key_filename='ssh-key.txt', username='soadev')
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('truncate --size 0 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out')

time.sleep(2)
# POST DATA to core service
headers = {'Content-type': 'application/xml'}
r = requests.post(url_coreservice_baru, data=req, headers=headers)
logger.debug(str(r.status_code) + '---------' + r.text)

# get The f log!
stdin, stdout, stderr = client.exec_command('tail -1048576 /opt/jboss-eap/bin/nohup.out | grep "ADAPTER BYTESTREAM"')

log = ""

for line in stdout:
log = line.strip('\n')

logger.debug(log)
i = log.find('003' + expectedBranch)
